  - Inherits from `Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig`\n   - Parses protobuf configuration into vector of header pairs\n\n2. **CustomHeaderInjectionFilter**: Main filter implementation\n   - Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` for request processing\n   - Implements `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` for response processing\n   - Injects headers in `decodeHeaders()` and `encodeHeaders()` methods\n\n3. **CustomHeaderInjectionConfig**: Factory class\n   - Inherits from `Common::FactoryBase`\n   - Creates filter instances from protobuf configuration\n   - Registered with Envoy's filter registry\n\n### Builds and runs the test suite\n\nAll BUILD files follow Envoy's standard patterns and use the appropriate build macros.\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n1. **Simple Iterator Pattern**: Uses traditional C++
